 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file:

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry living-room unknown-west - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; (connected kitchen living-room south)
    ; (door kitchen living-room south)
    (door laundry-room unknown-west west)
    (connected laundry-room unknown-west west)
  )
  (:goal
    (at unknown-west)
  )

 (define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at corridor)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; kitchen -> living-room (south, closed/unknown door)
    (door kitchen living-room south)
    (connected kitchen living-room south)
    ; corridor -> driveway (south, closed/unknown door)
    (door corridor driveway south)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; REMOVE: kitchen -> living-room (south, closed/unknown door) -- NO DOOR EXISTS
    ; corridor -> driveway (south, closed/unknown door)
    (door corridor driveway south)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at driveway)
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
 
 (define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor driveway living-room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; corridor -> driveway (south, unknown door state)
    (door corridor driveway south)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
    ; kitchen -> living-room (south, unknown door state)
    (door kitchen living-room south)
    (connected kitchen living-room south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

Parsed df and pf: 
 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
 
 (define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor driveway living-room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at corridor)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; REMOVE PREVIOUSLY ASSUMED DOOR BETWEEN CORRIDOR AND DRIVEWAY
    ; Only keep the visible connection for now.
  )
  (:goal
    (at driveway)
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
 
 (define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at corridor)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; corridor -> driveway (south, NO door defined, just connection seen)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at driveway)
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at corridor)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; Removed invalid connection from corridor to driveway
    ; Now only known valid rooms and connections are described
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; corridor -> south (driveway assumed behind corridor)
    (door corridor driveway south)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at driveway)
  )
)

Parsed df and pf: 
 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
 
 (define (problem explore-home)
  (:domain home-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room pantry corridor living-room driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at corridor)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited corridor)
    ; kitchen <-> laundry-room (north/south, open wood door)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (open kitchen laundry-room)
    (open laundry-room kitchen)
    (connected kitchen laundry-room north)
    (connected laundry-room kitchen south)
    ; kitchen <-> pantry (east/west, open frosted-glass door)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (open kitchen pantry)
    (open pantry kitchen)
    (connected kitchen pantry east)
    (connected pantry kitchen west)
    ; laundry-room <-> corridor (west/east, open wood door)
    (door laundry-room corridor west)
    (door corridor laundry-room east)
    (open laundry-room corridor)
    (open corridor laundry-room)
    (connected laundry-room corridor west)
    (connected corridor laundry-room east)
    ; kitchen <-> living-room (south/north, open path only seen, not an open door)
    (door kitchen living-room south)
    (door living-room kitchen north)
    (connected kitchen living-room south)
    (connected living-room kitchen north)
    ; corridor <-> driveway (south/north, only seen: no door, not open)
    (door corridor driveway south)
    (door driveway corridor north)
    (connected corridor driveway south)
    (connected driveway corridor north)
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?from - location ?to - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2)))
    :effect (open ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?to) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (connected ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
